  `Province` text NOT NULL,
  `Sector` text NOT NULL,

-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_mas_transport_topic definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_mas_transport_topic` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `LineNo` text NOT NULL,
  `Detail` text NOT NULL,
  `SubCtgCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `MenuDeptCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_mas_transport_subtopic definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_mas_transport_subtopic` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `SubLineNo` text NOT NULL,
  `SubDetails` text NOT NULL,
  `Topic_Id` int(150) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`),
  KEY `fk_transport_topic` (`Topic_Id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_transport_topic` FOREIGN KEY (`Topic_Id`) REFERENCES `tbl_mas_transport_topic` (`Id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_mas_transport_company definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_mas_transport_company` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `SupplierCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `SupplierName` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `Details` text NOT NULL,
  `Active` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `MenuDeptCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CompanyCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_trs_transport_doc definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_trs_transport_doc` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `NumberDoc` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `DocDate` date NOT NULL,
  `ReserveDate` date NOT NULL,
  `LoadDate` date NOT NULL,
  `TransportCompany` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `CategoryCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `Vehicle` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `LicensePlate` text NOT NULL,
  `DriverName` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `DriverTel` text NOT NULL,
  `AdminName` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `AdminTel` text NOT NULL,
  `StartTime` time NOT NULL,
  `EndTime` time NOT NULL,
  `DocHdNote` text NOT NULL,
  `StatusDoc` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `CompanyCode` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `MenuDeptCode` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_trs_transport_list definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_trs_transport_list` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `NumberDoc` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `LineNo` text NOT NULL,
  `InvoiceNo` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerCode` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerName` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `CustomerType` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `DeliverPlaceCode` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `Province` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `Sector` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `InvoiceAmount` text NOT NULL,
  `GoodsAmount` text NOT NULL,
  `InvoicePrice` text NOT NULL,
  `BillDate` text NOT NULL,
  `BillDoc` text NOT NULL,
  `CreateOn` text NOT NULL,
  `Round` int(150) NOT NULL,
  `IdRef` int(150) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `IsSAP` int(1) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`),
  KEY `fk_transport_list_doc` (`IdRef`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_transport_list_doc` FOREIGN KEY (`IdRef`) REFERENCES `tbl_trs_transport_doc` (`Id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;


-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_trs_transport_condition definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_trs_transport_condition` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `NumberDoc` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CompanyCode` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `MenuDeptCode` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `CategoryCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `SubCtgCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `TopicId` int(150) NOT NULL,
  `SubTopicId` int(150) NOT NULL,
  `Score` text,
  `Note` text NOT NULL,
  `IdRef` int(150) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_doc_subtopic` (`IdRef`,`SubTopicId`),
  KEY `fk_condition_topic` (`TopicId`),
  KEY `fk_condition_subtopic` (`SubTopicId`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_condition_subtopic` FOREIGN KEY (`SubTopicId`) REFERENCES `tbl_mas_transport_subtopic` (`Id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_condition_topic` FOREIGN KEY (`TopicId`) REFERENCES `tbl_mas_transport_topic` (`Id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_transport_condition_doc` FOREIGN KEY (`IdRef`) REFERENCES `tbl_trs_transport_doc` (`Id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- chaosuawebapp.tbl_mas_transport_customer definition

CREATE TABLE `tbl_mas_transport_customer` (
  `Id` int(150) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ListCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `ListName` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `ListType` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `Details` text NOT NULL,
  `Active` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `MenuDeptCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CompanyCode` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `CreateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `CreateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UpdateBy` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `UpdateDateTime` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`Id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
